if(cyberCountdownModule.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; typeof rawcfg !== 'undefined') {
var cfg = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(rawcfg));

var $hours1 = cyberCountdownModule.find('.js-coutdown-h1');
var $hours2 = cyberCountdownModule.find('.js-coutdown-h2');
var $minutes1 = cyberCountdownModule.find('.js-coutdown-m1');
var $minutes2 = cyberCountdownModule.find('.js-coutdown-m2');
var $seconds1 = cyberCountdownModule.find('.js-coutdown-s1');
var $seconds2 = cyberCountdownModule.find('.js-coutdown-s2');

  //ADD LEADING ZERO FUNCTION

   function addLeadingZero(timeDigit) {

    var leadingZeroTimeDigit = timeDigit;

    if (leadingZeroTimeDigit &lt; 10) {

      leadingZeroTimeDigit = '0' + leadingZeroTimeDigit;

    }

    // Turn this number into a string so we can use its composite parts
    // in the updateCountdown method
    return leadingZeroTimeDigit.toString();

  }


// PARSE DATE FUNCTION
  function parseDatetime(serialisedDate) {
    const YEAR = 1;
    const MONTH = 2;
    const DAY = 3;
    const HOUR = 4;
    const MINUTE = 5;
    const SECOND = 6;
    const data = /(\d+)-(\d+)-(\d+)\s(\d+):(\d+):(\d+)/.exec(serialisedDate);

    return new Date(
      data[YEAR],
      data[MONTH] - 1,
      data[DAY],
      data[HOUR],
      data[MINUTE],
      data[SECOND]
    );
  };




//UPDATE COUNTDOWN FUNCTION
  function updateCountdown(secondsLeft) {
    // Split the time into HH:MM:SS with leading zeroes
    var
      hours = parseInt(secondsLeft / 3600, 10),
      minutes = parseInt(secondsLeft / 60, 10) % 60,
      seconds = secondsLeft % 60;

    // Update the values

    // Hours
    $hours1.text(addLeadingZero(hours)[0]);
    $hours2.text(addLeadingZero(hours)[1]);

    // Minutes
    $minutes1.text(addLeadingZero(minutes)[0]);
    $minutes2.text(addLeadingZero(minutes)[1]);

    // Seconds
    $seconds1.text(addLeadingZero(seconds)[0]);
    $seconds2.text(addLeadingZero(seconds)[1]);

  }

//START COUNTDOWN FUNCTION

 function startCountdown(timeLeft) {
    var deadLineTime = parseDatetime(timeLeft).getTime();
    var currentTime = new Date().getTime();
    var secondsLeftNow = (deadLineTime - currentTime) / 1000;

    var _timer = setInterval(function () {
      if (secondsLeftNow &gt;= 0) {
        updateCountdown(secondsLeftNow);
        secondsLeftNow--;
      } else {
        updateCountdown(0);
        clearInterval(_timer);
      }
    }, 1000);
  }


 startCountdown(cfg.timerExpiresIn);


}


}
